					var getCookieValue = function(key) {
						var binfo=document.cookie.split(";");
						var tmp="";
						for (var i=0; i<binfo.length; i++) {
							if (binfo[i].indexOf(key)>=0) {
								tmp=binfo[i].substring(binfo[i].indexOf("=")+1,binfo[i].length);
								break;
							}
						}
						return tmp;
					};

					var eleveniaSwitcher = function () {
						var options = {mode: 'desktop', cookieName: 'SWITCH_TYPE'};
						var redirectionMap = { 
							mobile: ["/category/getLargeProductList.do", "/category/getMiddleProductList.do", "/product/getProductDetail.do", "/register/certification.do", "/register/birthday.do", "/member/unsubscribe/newsletter.do", "/Corner/getExhibitionFrontDetail.do", "/Corner/getFeaturedItem.do", "/Corner/getDailyDeals.do", "/Corner/new-deals/main.do", "/Corner/brand-deals/main.do", "/event/promotionList.do", "/html/promo.html", "/html/deals.html", "/html/top100.html"],

						var redirectException = ["/connect/GatewayAction/Xsite.do", "/connect/GatewayAction/getTid.do"];
						var cookieMap = {mobile: "MW", desktop: "WB"};
						var shouldRedirect = function (path) {
							if (checkArrayIndexOf(redirectException, path) > -1) {
								return false;
							}

							var cookieValue = getCookieValue(options.cookieName);
							if (cookieValue != '') {
								if (cookieValue == cookieMap[options.mode]) {
									return false;
								} else {
									if (cookieValue == "WB" && options.mode == 'mobile') {
										return true;
									} else if (cookieValue == "MW" && options.mode == 'desktop') {
										return true;
									}
								}
							} else {
								if (mobileDetector.isAndroidTablet() || mobileDetector.isIpad()) {
									return false;
								}
								if (mobileDetector.isMobileBrowser() || mobileDetector.isApp() || mobileDetector.isOperaMobile()) {
									return true;
								}
							}
							return false;
						};
						
						return {
							execute: function () {
								var path = location.pathname;
								var queryIndex = path.indexOf('>');
								if (queryIndex > -1) {

    setGnbCtgrGrp();
$(document).ready(function($) {
	function nonFloatMenuBigBannerGap(thisImage){
		try{				
			var trcNo = $(thisImage).attr("data-trcno");
			var imgAlt=$(thisImage).attr("alt");
			var gapPosition= "1";
			
			if(typeof trcNo != 'undefined'){
				var gapPromoObj ={
						'name' : imgAlt,
						'id': trcNo,
						'creative':'Main Page - Menu Non Float',
						'position':gapPosition
				};
				
				var params = {"promoList":[gapPromoObj]};				
				if(typeof gap !="undefined"){
					gap.setPromotionImpression(params);						
				}	
			}
									
		}catch(e){}	
	}
	for(var i=1; i<=8; i++){
		$('.layNavCate'+i+'Lazy').parent().hover(function() {
			$(this).find("img").lazyload({placeholder:loadingImg,load:function(){nonFloatMenuBigBannerGap(this);}});
			var disp = $(this).find("div[id^='layNavCate']").css("display");
			if(disp=="block"){
				$(this).find("a[class='nav-item']").addClass("on");
			} else {
				$(this).find("a[class='nav-item on']").removeClass("on");
			}
		});
	}
});
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    if(typeof(billBoardListTab) != "undefined" && billBoardListTab.DATA != null && billBoardListTab.DATA.length > 0) {
		try {
			(function(){
			    var mainBillboard = new MainBillboard();
	    		window.attachEvent ? window.attachEvent('onload', mainBillboard.init()) : window.addEventListener('load', mainBillboard.init(), false);
			})();

	/* Tracking Main Billboard Banner */
	var bannerLink = $('#ulBannerList .main-banner-inner a');

	$(bannerLink).click(function(event) {
	  var url = $(this).attr('href');
	  var path = url.substr(url.indexOf('/', 7) + 1);
	  var imgAlt = $(this).find('img').attr('alt');
	  var imgBnrId = $(this).find('img').attr('data-trcno');
	  var imgTab = $(this).parents('li').attr('id');
	  
	  var cb = generate_callback($(this));
	  event.preventDefault();
	  
	  mixpanel.track("CLICK_BANNER", { 
	    "Banner_ID": imgBnrId,
	    "Banner_Title": imgAlt,
	    "Banner_Position": imgTab,
	    "URL" : url
	    }, cb);
	  setTimeout(cb, 500);
	});
	
	function generate_callback(a) {
	    return function() {
	        window.location = a.attr("href");
	    }
	}
	/* end Tracking Main Billboard Banner */
   </script>

	// historical
	 function setHistoricalPulsa(){
		
		//alert('setHistoricalPulsa');
		
		if(funcCheckIsLogin()){
			//alert("funcCheckIsLogin true");
			var msisdnTo = pulsahistMap['100'];
			var dataTo = pulsahistMap['200'];
			var plnTo = pulsahistMap['300'];
			
			if(msisdnTo != ""){
				$("#pulsaInputPhone").val(msisdnTo);
				var pulsaTag = $("#pulsaInputPhone")[0];
				//var pulsaTag = document.getElementById("pulsaInputPhone");
				//alert(pulsaTag.val());
				checkOperatorPrefix(pulsaTag);
			}
			
			if(dataTo != ""){
				$("#dataInputPhone").val(dataTo);
				var dataTag = $("#dataInputPhone")[0];
				//var dataTag = document.getElementById("dataInputPhone");
				//alert(dataTag.val());
				checkOperatorPrefix(dataTag);
			}
			
			if(plnTo != ""){
				$("#plnInputPhone").val(plnTo);
			}
		}
		
	} 
	
	/* SMS-OTP start */
	function openSmsOtpPopUp(){
		
		buyTopUpProcessing = false;
		
		$.ajax({
	        type: 'GET',
	        url: '/instantpay/smsotp/getSmsOtpInfo.do',
	        dataType: 'json',
	        async:   true,
	        success: function(data) {
	        	if(data.responseCode == "SUCCESS"){
	        		$('#memberHpNo').html(data.memberHpNo);
	        		$('#trxId').val(data.trxId);
	        		
	        		// show sms otp popup
	        		jQuery("#smsOtpPopupId", document).show();
	        	    $("#smsOtpPopupId").css("display","block");
	        	}
			},
	        error: function(xhr) {
	            alert("Ada kesalahan sistem. Silahkan hubungi customer service kami.");
	        }
	    });
	    
	    //jQuery("#dimmedSmsOtp", document).show();
	}

	function closeSmsOtpPopUp(){
		
		buyTopUpProcessing = false;
		
		$('#memberHpNo').html("");
		$('#trxId').val("");
		$('#otpNumber').val("");
		
		jQuery("#smsOtpPopupId", document).hide();
	    $("#smsOtpPopupId").css("display","none");
	}

	function validateSmsOtpPopUp(){
		$.ajax({
	        type: 'GET',
	        url: '/instantpay/smsotp/getSmsOtpInfo.do',
	        dataType: 'json',
	        async:   true,
	        success: function(data) {
	        	if(data.responseCode == "SUCCESS"){
	        		$('#memberHpNo').html(data.memberHpNo);
	        		$('#trxId').val(data.trxId);
	        		
	        		// show sms otp popup
	        		jQuery("#smsOtpPopupId", document).show();
	        	    $("#smsOtpPopupId").css("display","block");
	        	}
			},
	        error: function(xhr) {
	            alert("Ada kesalahan sistem. Silahkan hubungi customer service kami.");
	        }
	    });
	}

	function retrySmsOtpPopUp(){
		
		var otpNumber = $('#otpNumber').val();
		
		$.ajax({
	        type: 'GET',
	        url: '/instantpay/smsotp/getSmsOtpInfo.do',
	        dataType: 'json',
	        data:{otpNumber:otpNumber},
	        async:   true,
	        success: function(data) {
	        	if(data.responseCode == "SUCCESS"){        		
	        		// show sms otp popup
	        		jQuery("#smsOtpPopupId", document).show();
	        	    $("#smsOtpPopupId").css("display","block");
	        	}else if(data.responseCode == "E02"){
	        		openMaxOtpReqPopup();
	        	}
			},
	        error: function(xhr) {
	            alert("Ada kesalahan sistem. Silahkan hubungi customer service kami.");
	        }
	    });
	}

	function openWrongInputOtpPopup(){
		jQuery("#smsOtpPopupId", document).hide();
	    $("#smsOtpPopupId").css("display","none");
		
		jQuery("#wrongInputOtpPopupId", document).show();
	    $("#wrongInputOtpPopupId").css("display","block");
	}

	function closeWrongInputOtpPopup(){
		$('#otpNumber').val("");
		
		jQuery("#smsOtpPopupId", document).show();
	    $("#smsOtpPopupId").css("display","block");
		
		jQuery("#wrongInputOtpPopupId", document).hide();
	    $("#wrongInputOtpPopupId").css("display","none");
	}

	function openMaxOtpReqPopup(){
		jQuery("#smsOtpPopupId", document).hide();
	    $("#smsOtpPopupId").css("display","none");
		
		jQuery("#maxOtpReqPopupId", document).show();
	    $("#maxOtpReqPopupId").css("display","block");
	}

	function closeMaxOtpReqPopup(){	
		jQuery("#maxOtpReqPopupId", document).hide();
	    $("#maxOtpReqPopupId").css("display","none");
	    
	    closeSmsOtpPopUp();
	}

		jQuery("#smsOtpPopupId", document).hide();
	    $("#smsOtpPopupId").css("display","none");
	    
		jQuery("#expiredOtpPopupId", document).show();
	    $("#expiredOtpPopupId").css("display","block");
	}

	    $("#smsOtpPopupId").css("display","block");
		
		jQuery("#expiredOtpPopupId", document).hide();
	    $("#expiredOtpPopupId").css("display","none");
	}

        type: 'GET',
        url: '/browsing/PulsaMain/getPulsaHistoryMap.do',
        dataType: 'json',
        data:{},
        success: function(data) {
        	if(data!=null){
        		pulsahistMapCallBack(data.responseBody);
        	}else{
        		pulsahistMap["100"] = "";
        		pulsahistMap["200"] = "";
        		pulsahistMap["300"] = "";
        	}
        },
        error: function(xhr) {
        	pulsahistMap["100"] = "";
    		pulsahistMap["200"] = "";
    		pulsahistMap["300"] = "";
        }
	});
	
	function onlyNumberV2(val) 
	{
		var strValue = $.trim(val);
		
		if (isNaN(strValue) || strValue=='' || strValue ==null) {
			return false;
		}
		
		return true;
	}
	
	
	function onlyNumber(frmNm) 
	{
		var strValue = $.trim(frmNm.value);
		if (isNaN(strValue)) {
			//alert("Anda hanya bisa menggunakan angka.");
			//frmNm.value = strValue.replace(/\D/g,'');
			//frmNm.focus();
			$(frmNm).addClass("redAlert");
			return false;
		}
		return true;
	}
	
	var previGroup100OperatorCode = ""; // check if the same , no need to call nominal list (triggered by keyup and onchange for input)
	var previGroup200OperatorCode = "";
	var selectedAquaProduct = "";

	function checkOperatorPrefix(thisSel){
		var checkResult = false;
		var inputPhoneNo = $.trim(thisSel.value);
		var dtlsCd = $(thisSel).data("dtlscd");		
		
		
		if(inputPhoneNo != ""){
			var inputPhoneNoPrefix1 = inputPhoneNo.substring(0,4);
			var inputPhoneNoPrefix2 = inputPhoneNo.substring(0,5);
			var inputPhoneNoPrefix3 = inputPhoneNo.substring(0,3);
			
			for(var i = 0 ; i < operatorPhonePrefixList.length; i++){				
				var operatorPhoneObj = operatorPhonePrefixList[i];
				var prefixListString = operatorPhoneObj.prefixNo;			
				var groupCode = operatorPhoneObj.group;
				
				if(groupCode == dtlsCd && groupCode != "300"){
					var operatorCode = operatorPhoneObj.operator;
					
					if(checkMatchingPrefix(inputPhoneNoPrefix1,inputPhoneNoPrefix2,inputPhoneNoPrefix3,prefixListString)){
						
						if(operatorCssMap.hasOwnProperty(operatorCode)){
							resetPulsaPaketPln(thisSel,"input");
							$(thisSel).addClass(operatorCssMap[operatorCode]);
							 
						}
						
						var needCallNominalList = false;
						if(groupCode == "100"){
							var nominalOptLength = $(".pulsaNominalSel option").length;
							if( previGroup100OperatorCode != operatorCode || nominalOptLength <=1){
								needCallNominalList = true;
								previGroup100OperatorCode = operatorCode;
							}
							
						}else if(groupCode == "200" ){
							var nominalOptLength = $(".paketNominalSel option").length;
							if(previGroup200OperatorCode != operatorCode || nominalOptLength <=1){
								needCallNominalList = true;
								previGroup200OperatorCode = operatorCode;
							}							
						}
						
						if(!needCallNominalList || (needCallNominalList && setNominalList(groupCode, operatorCode))){							
							checkResult = true;
							$(thisSel).removeClass("redAlert");
							break;
						}											
						
					}else{						
						/* showRedAlert(inputPhoneNo, operatorPhonePrefixList, checkResult, dtlsCd, i);
						resetPulsaPaketPln(thisSel); */
					}
				}else{
					/* showRedAlert(inputPhoneNo, operatorPhonePrefixList, checkResult, dtlsCd,i);
					resetPulsaPaketPln(thisSel); */
				}
				
			}
			
		}
		
		if(checkResult == false){
			resetPulsaPaketPln(thisSel,"all");
			showRedAlert(inputPhoneNo, checkResult, dtlsCd);
			
		}
		
		return checkResult;
	}	
	
	function showRedAlert(inputPhoneNo, checkResult, dtlsCd){
		var firstTwoPrefix = inputPhoneNo.substring(0,2);						
		
		//if(index == (operatorPhonePrefixList.length - 1) && checkResult == false){ // if still has next, do not show alert, continue checking until last index then show alert
			if((firstTwoPrefix != "62" && inputPhoneNo.length <= 4) || (firstTwoPrefix == "62" && inputPhoneNo.length >= 5) || inputPhoneNo.length > 5){
				if(dtlsCd == "100"){
					$("#pulsaInputPhone").addClass("redAlert");
				}else if(dtlsCd == "200"){
					$("#dataInputPhone").addClass("redAlert");
				}
			}	
		//}
	}
	
	function resetPulsaPaketPln(thisSel,section){
		var dtlsCd = $(thisSel).data("dtlscd");
		if(section == "all" || section == "nominal"){
			if(dtlsCd == "100"){
				$(".pulsaNominalSel option:first:first-child").siblings().remove();
				$(".pls-price .prc").not(":hidden").removeClass("active").html("Rp -");
				$(".btn-buy").not(":hidden").removeClass("active");
			}else if(dtlsCd == "200"){
				$(".paketNominalSel option:first:first-child").siblings().remove();
				$(".pls-price .prc").not(":hidden").removeClass("active").html("Rp -");
				$(".btn-buy").not(":hidden").removeClass("active");
			}else if(dtlsCd == "400"){
				$(".gameNominalSel option:first-child").siblings().remove();
				$(".pls-price .prc").not(":hidden").removeClass("active").html("Rp -");
				$(".btn-buy").not(":hidden").removeClass("active");
			}else if(dtlsCd == "600"){
				$(".donateNominalSel option:first-child").siblings().remove();
				$(".pls-price .prc").not(":hidden").removeClass("active").html("Rp -");
				$(".btn-buy").not(":hidden").removeClass("active");
			}
		}
		
		if(section == "all" || section == "input"){
			if($(thisSel).hasClass("redAlert")){
				$(thisSel).removeClass();
				$(thisSel).addClass("redAlert");
			}else{
				$(thisSel).removeClass();
			}
		}
		
		
	}
	
	function resetPayInstant(){
		$(".cboxInstPay").not(":hidden").prop("checked",false);
		$(".btn-buy").not(":hidden").html("Beli Sekarang");
		var $instPay = $(".pls-instpay").not(":hidden");
		var $msgTop = $instPay.find(".msgTop");
		$msgTop.html("").hide();
	}
	
	function validateTagihanBeforeSubmit(){

		var tagihanParent = $('#selTagihan').val();
		var tagihanSub = $('#selTagihanPrd').val();
		
		if( tagihanParent==null || tagihanParent==''){
			alert("Harap pilih jenis tagihan !");
			$('#selTagihan').focus();
			return false;
		}
		
		if( tagihanSub==null || tagihanSub==''){
			alert("Harap pilih produk tagihan !");
			$('#selTagihanPrd').focus();
			return false;
		}
		
		return true;
	}
	
	function getPrefix(parmInp){
		var parmNo = "";
		if(parmInp.substring(0,1)=="0" && parmInp.length>3){
			parmNo = parmInp.substring(0,4);
		}else if(parmInp.substring(0,2)=="62" && parmInp.length>4){
			parmNo = parmInp.substring(0,5);
		}else if(parmInp.substring(0,3)=="999" && parmInp.length>2){
			parmNo = parmInp.substring(0,3);
		}
		return parmNo;
	}
	
	function hideErrorTagihan(){

		$('#tagihanErr span').html("");

		$('#tagihanErr').hide();

		$('a#tagihanBtnPay').css("margin-top","25px");
	} 
	
	function displayErrorTagihan(){
		$('#tagihanErr span').css("color","#ff0000");
		$('#tagihanErr').css("display","block");
		$('#tagihanErr').css("margin-left","5px");
		$('a#tagihanBtnPay').css("margin-top","0px");
		$('#tagihanMemberId').focus();
	}
	
	function setBillerLogo(prefix,dtlscd){
		clearBackgroundTagihan();

		
		var tagihanParent 	= $('#selTagihan').val();
		var tagihanSub 		= $('#selTagihanPrd').val();
		var prefixParm      = getPrefix(prefix);
			if( dtlscd =="800" && tagihanParent!=''  ){

				
				if(	validateTagihanBeforeSubmit()){

				
					if(tagihanParent=='800'){ //PLN

						setOperatorPLNPostPaid();
					
					}else if(tagihanParent=='801'){	//BPJS
					
						setOperatorBPJSPostPaid();
					
					}else if(tagihanParent=='802'){	//PDAM
						
						setOperatorPDAMPostPaid();
					
					}else if(tagihanParent=='803'){ //PASCA MOBILE
						
						getOperatorDetail(prefixParm,dtlscd);
					
					}else if(tagihanParent=='804'){ //INTERNET
						
						if(tagihanSub =='8041'){
							
							setOperatorCBNPostPaid();	//CBN
						}
					
						if(tagihanSub =='8042'){
							
							setOperatorTELKOMPostPaid(); //TELKOM PSTN & INDIHOME
							
						}
					}
					
				 }
			}
		
	}
	
	function setOperatorMobilePostPaid( operator ){
		if(operator != ""){
			if(operatorCssMap.hasOwnProperty(operator)){

				 $(".tabTagihan input.opCode").addClass(operatorCssMap[operator]);
			}
		}
	}
	
	function getOperatorDetail(opCode,dtlscd){
		if(dtlscd!="700"){
			$.ajax({
		        type: 'GET',
		        url: '/browsing/PulsaMain/getOperatorDetail.do',
		        dataType: 'json',
		        data:{opCode:opCode , dtlscd:dtlscd},
		        async:   true,
		        success: function(data) {
		        	if(data!=null && data.result == "00"){
		
		        		if(data.operatorList!=null && data.operatorList.length>0){
		        			var group = data.operatorList[0].group;
		        			var operator = (typeof(data.operatorList[0].operator)=="undefined") ? null : data.operatorList[0].operator;
		        
		        			if(dtlscd =='800'){
		        				
		        				if(group =="803"){
			        					setOperatorMobilePostPaid(operator);
			        			}
		        			}
		        			
		        		}
		        	}else{
		        		alert("Operator tidak tersedia");
		        	}
				},
		        error: function(xhr) {
		            alert("Ada kesalahan sistem. Silahkan hubungi customer service kami.");
		        }
		    });
		}
	}
	
	function checkMatchingPrefix(inputPhoneNoPrefix1,inputPhoneNoPrefix2,inputPhoneNoPrefix3, prefixListString){
		var matchResult = false;
		if(prefixListString != ""){			
			var prefixListArr = prefixListString.split("|");		
			for(var i=0 ; i < prefixListArr.length ;i++){
				var prefixNo = prefixListArr[i];
				if(prefixNo == inputPhoneNoPrefix1 || prefixNo == inputPhoneNoPrefix2 || prefixNo == inputPhoneNoPrefix3){
					matchResult = true;
					break;
				}
			}			
		}		
		return matchResult;
	}

	var tempPhoneNo="";
	function validatePhoneNo(thisSel,event){
		var inputPhoneNo = $.trim(thisSel.value);
		var firstTwoPrefix = inputPhoneNo.substring(0,2);
		var firstThreePrefix = inputPhoneNo.substring(0,3);
		
		if(onlyNumber(thisSel) == false){
			return false;
		}
		
		if(event.keyCode != 8 && event.keyCode != 46 && tempPhoneNo != inputPhoneNo){
			if((inputPhoneNo.length == 4 || (inputPhoneNo.length == 5 && firstTwoPrefix == "62") || (inputPhoneNo.length == 3 && firstThreePrefix == "999")) && checkOperatorPrefix(thisSel) == false){
				return false;
			}
		}else if(inputPhoneNo.length < 3 || (firstTwoPrefix == "08" && inputPhoneNo.length < 4) || (firstTwoPrefix == "62" && inputPhoneNo.length < 5)){
			resetPulsaPaketPln(thisSel,"all");
		}
		
		tempPhoneNo = inputPhoneNo;
	}
	
	
	var actionTypeAfterLogin = "";
	
	function actionForLoginOK() {
	    jQuery('body').removeClass('overH');
	    $("#loginpopup").attr("src","");
	    jQuery("iframe[name='layerIframe']").hide();
		jQuery(".dimmed").remove();		
		
	    if(typeof setGnbLoginArea == "function" && funcCheckIsLogin() && typeof CP_IS_AUTH != "undefined"){	    	
    		CP_IS_AUTH =  true;
    		setGnbLoginArea();	
	    }
	    if(actionTypeAfterLogin == "isi-pulsa"){
	    	topUpBuyNow();	    	
	    }else if(actionTypeAfterLogin == "point-refill"){
	    	fnTopUpSubmit();	    	
	    }
	    
	    actionTypeAfterLogin = "";
	}
	
	var popUpLogin = function(actionType){
		if (typeof openLoginPopup != "undefined"){
			openLoginPopup("01");	
			actionTypeAfterLogin = actionType;
			$("#loginpopup").css("z-index","99999999");
		}
	}
	
	var selectedNominalSeq = "";
	var buyTopUpProcessing = false;	
	
	function topUpBuyNow(){
		var $cboxInstPay = $(".cboxInstPay").not(":hidden");
		if(buyTopUpProcessing === true){
			alert("Pembelian top-up sedang diproses. Mohon ditunggu.");
		}else if(!funcCheckIsLogin()){
			alert("Silahkan login terlebih dahulu.");
			//login();
			popUpLogin("isi-pulsa");
		}else if($cboxInstPay.is(":checked") && !checkBuyInstStatus()){
			
		}else{
			buyTopUpProcessing = true;
			if(validateForm()){				
				var form = document.frmMain;
				
				if(selectedNominalSeq != ""){				
					$.ajax({
				        type: 'GET',
				        url: '/browsing/PulsaMain/getProductDetail.do',
				        dataType: 'json',
				        data:{seq: selectedNominalSeq, eCouponSms1:$("#eCouponSms1").val(), eCouponSms2:$("#eCouponSms2").val()},
				        async: true,
				        success: function(data) {
				        	if(data!=null && data.result == "00"){
				        		//set parameter
								form.elements.prdNo.value =  data.prdNo;
								form.elements.mstrPrdNo.value =  data.mstrPrdNo;
								form.elements.selMthdCd.value =  data.selMthdCd;
								form.elements.dispCtgrNo.value =  data.dispCtgrNo;
								form.elements.ldispCtgrNo.value =  data.ldispCtgrNo;
								form.elements.bsnDealClf.value =  data.bsnDealClf;
								form.elements.optCnt.value =  "1";
								form.elements.optionStock.value = "1";//QUANTITY
								form.elements.selMnbdNo.value =  data.selMnbdNo;
								form.elements.mobileYn.value =  data.mobileYn;
								form.elements.selPrc.value =  data.selPrc;
								form.elements.iscpn.value =  data.iscpn;
								form.elements.selStatCd.value =  data.selStatCd;
								form.elements.optionStckNo.value =  data.optionStckNo;
								form.elements.optionPrc.value =  data.optionPrc;
								form.elements.optionStockHid.value =  data.optionStockHid;
								form.elements.dlvDtlsMthdCd.value =  data.dlvDtlsMthdCd;
								form.elements.dlvMthdCd.value =  data.dlvMthdCd;
								form.elements.optionStockHid.value =  data.totStock;
								form.elements.optionStckNo.value =  data.totPrdStckNo;
								form.elements.optionPrc.value =  data.totPrdPrc;
								form.elements.prdMinorYn.value =  data.prdMinorYn;	
								form.elements.eCouponEmail.value =  data.memId;
								
								//submit!
								form.action = _SSL_ACTION_CONTEXT_URL_ + "/pay/newOrderStep1/getOrderInfo.do";
								form.elements.isFast.value = "Y";
								form.elements.isPopup.value = "N";
								form.elements.isSSL.value = "Y";
								
								if($(".cboxInstPay").not(":hidden").is(":checked")){
									form.elements.payInstantYN.value = "Y";
									if(phoneVerifiedYN == "Y"){
										// SMS-OTP start
										var trxId = form.elements.trxId.value;
										if(trxId != ""){
											var otpNumber = $('#otpNumbInputVal').val();
											if(otpNumber != "" && !isNaN(otpNumber)){
												form.elements.otpNumber.value = otpNumber;
												topUpBuyNowInstPay();
											}else{
												alert("Wrong Format or Empty");	
											}	
										}else{
											//buyTopUpProcessing = false;
											openSmsOtpPopUp();
										}
										// SMS-OTP end
									}else{
										form.elements.phoneVerifiedYN.value = "N";
										form.submit();
									}										
								}else{
									form.elements.payInstantYN.value = "N";
									form.submit();
								}
								
				        	}else if(data!=null && data.result == "01"){ //XOP-11785
				        		alert(data.msg);
				        		buyTopUpProcessing = false;
				        		location.href=data.redirectUrl;
				        	}else{
				        		alert(data.msg);
				        		buyTopUpProcessing = false;
				        	}
						},
				        error: function(xhr) {
				            alert("Ada kesalahan sistem. Silahkan hubungi customer service kami.");
				            buyTopUpProcessing = false;
				        }
				    });
				}else{
					buyTopUpProcessing = false;
				}
			}else{
				buyTopUpProcessing = false;
			}
			
			
		}		
		
	}

		if(!funcCheckIsLogin()){
	    	alert("Silahkan login terlebih dahulu.");
			openLoginPopup('02');	
		}
		else{
			var form = document.frmMain;

			if(validateForm()){
				afterAquaAgreement();
			}
		}
	}

		$.ajax({

		});
		
	};
	
	function openPayInstThxPop(){
		var $payInstThx = $(".payInstThx");
		var payInstDimmed = "<div class=\"dimmed payInstDimmed\" style=\"opacity: 0.4;display:block\"></div>";
		$("body").append(payInstDimmed);
		$payInstThx.show();
	}
	
	function closePayInstThxPop(){
		var $payInstThx = $(".payInstThx");
		$payInstThx.hide();
		$('.payInstDimmed').remove();
		location.reload();
	}
	
	function topUpBuyNowInstPay(){
		//SMS-OTP
		jQuery("#smsOtpPopupId", document).hide();
	    $("#smsOtpPopupId").css("display","none");
		
		var form = document.frmMain;
		//var data = {"result" : "00", "prdGroup":"300", "ordNo" :"982391233" ,"selPrc" :"54.900", "rcvrNm" : "Cokrominoto", "rcvrTlphn": "0812-1262373", "prdNm" :"XL/Paket/PLN vs Tv/Game/Donation Prd Nm"};
		//$(".loadingCheckOut").show();
		$.ajax({
	        type: 'POST',
	        url: "/pay/newOrderStep1/getOrderInfo.do",
	        dataType: 'json',
	        data: $(form).serialize(),
	        async: true,
	        beforeSend: function(){
	        	$(".loadingCheckOut").show();
	        },
	        success: function(data) {
	        	if(data.result == "00"){
	        		
	        		//SMS-OTP
	        		closeSmsOtpPopUp();
	        		
	        		var prdGroup = data.prdGroup;
	        		var $instPhoneRow = $(".instPhoneRow");
	        		var $instAccNoRow =$(".instAccNoRow");
	        		var $instPhone=$(".instPhone");
	        		var $instAccNo=$(".instAccNo");
	        		var $instMsg=$(".instMsg");
	        		
	        		$(".instOrdNo").html(data.ordNo);
	        		$(".instRcvrNm").html(data.rcvrNm);
	        		$(".instPrice").html("Rp "+numberComma(data.selPrc));
	        		$(".instPrdNm").html(data.prdNm);
	        		$instPhoneRow.hide();
	        		$instAccNoRow.hide();
	        		
	        		if(prdGroup == "100"){
	        			$instMsg.html("Anda akan menerima SMS dari operator anda jika pulsa telah berhasil terisi.");
	        			$instPhone.html(data.rcvrTlphn);	        			
	        			$instPhoneRow.show();
	        		}else if (prdGroup == "200"){
	        			$instMsg.html("Anda akan menerima SMS dari operator anda jika paket data telah berhasil terisi");
	        			$instPhone.html(data.rcvrTlphn);	        			
	        			$instPhoneRow.show();
	        		}else if (prdGroup == "300"){
	        			$instMsg.html("Anda akan menerima nomor token PLN melalui SMS dari elevenia atau melalui halaman my elevenia");
	        			$instAccNo.html(data.rcvrTlphn);	        			
	        			$instAccNoRow.show();
	        		}else if (prdGroup =="400" || prdGroup == "500" || prdGroup == "600"){
	        			$instMsg.html("Anda dapat memeriksa detail informasi pesanan/pembayaran anda di halaman My elevenia.");			
	        			if(prdGroup == "500"){
	        				$instAccNo.html(data.rcvrTlphn);				
	        				$instAccNoRow.show();
	        			}else{
	        				$instPhone.html(data.rcvrTlphn);				
	        				$instPhoneRow.show();
	        			}
	        		}
	        		openPayInstThxPop();
	        		buyTopUpProcessing = false;	
	        	//SMS-OTP start
	        	}else if(data.result == "E02"){
	        		openMaxOtpReqPopup();
	        	}else if(data.result == "E04"){
	        		openWrongInputOtpPopup();
	        	}else if(data.result == "E05"){
	        		openExpiredOtpPopup();
	        	}else if(data.result == "E500"){
	        		e500Response();
	        	//SMS-OTP end
	        	}else{
	        		alert(data.msg);
	        		buyTopUpProcessing = false;	
	        	}
	        	
			},
			complete:function(data){
				$(".loadingCheckOut").hide();
				buyTopUpProcessing = false;	
			},
	        error: function(xhr) {
	            alert("Ada kesalahan sistem. Silahkan hubungi customer service kami.");
	        } 
		});
	}
	
	function setFormPhoneNumber(inputPhoneNo){
		var firstTwoPrefix = inputPhoneNo.substring(0,2);	
		var firstThreePrefix = inputPhoneNo.substring(0,3);
		var inputPhoneNoPrefix1 ="";
		var inputPhoneNoPrefix2 ="";
		if(firstTwoPrefix == "62" && inputPhoneNo.length >= 5){
			inputPhoneNoPrefix1 = "0"+inputPhoneNo.substring(2,5);
			inputPhoneNoPrefix2 = inputPhoneNo.substring(5,inputPhoneNo.length);			
		}else if(firstTwoPrefix == "08" && inputPhoneNo.length >= 4){
			inputPhoneNoPrefix1 = inputPhoneNo.substring(0,4);
			inputPhoneNoPrefix2 = inputPhoneNo.substring(4,inputPhoneNo.length);
		}else if(firstThreePrefix == "999"){//bolt
			inputPhoneNoPrefix1 = inputPhoneNo.substring(0,3);
			inputPhoneNoPrefix2 = inputPhoneNo.substring(3,inputPhoneNo.length);
		}
		$("#eCouponSms1").val(inputPhoneNoPrefix1);
		$("#eCouponSms2").val(inputPhoneNoPrefix2);
		
	}
	
	function validateForm(){
		var validationResult = false;
		
		var activeClassTab = $('.tab-nav li.active').find("a").data("tab");
		
		var nonSplitNumber = "";
		
		if(activeClassTab == "tabPulsa"){
			var $input = $("#pulsaInputPhone");
			var inputPhoneNo = $.trim($input.val());
			var nominalSelect = $.trim($(".pulsaNominalSel").val());
			
			if(inputPhoneNo == ""){
				alert("Masukkan No Handphone Anda.");
				$input.addClass("redAlert");
				return validationResult;
			}
			
			if(inputPhoneNo.length < 10){
				alert("Minimum nomor telepon adalah 10 angka.");
				$input.addClass("redAlert");
				return validationResult;
			}
			
			if(onlyNumber($input.get(0)) == false){
				$input.addClass("redAlert");
				return validationResult;
			}
						
			if(nominalSelect == ""){
				alert("Silahkan Pilih Pulsa Nominal.");
				return validationResult;
			}
			validationResult = true;
			setFormPhoneNumber(inputPhoneNo);			
			selectedNominalSeq = nominalSelect;
			
		}else if(activeClassTab == "tabData"){
			var $input = $("#dataInputPhone");
			var inputPhoneNo = $.trim($input.val());
			var nominalSelect = $.trim($(".paketNominalSel").val());
			
			if(inputPhoneNo == ""){
				alert("Masukkan No Handphone Anda.");
				$input.addClass("redAlert");
				return validationResult;
			}
			
			if(inputPhoneNo.length < 10){
				alert("Minimum nomor telepon yang Anda masukan adalah 10 angka.");
				$input.addClass("redAlert");
				return validationResult;
			}
			
			if(onlyNumber($input.get(0)) == false){
				$input.addClass("redAlert");
				return validationResult;
			}
						
			if(nominalSelect == ""){
				alert("Silahkan Pilih Nominal Paket Data.");
				return validationResult;
			}
			validationResult = true;
			setFormPhoneNumber(inputPhoneNo);
			selectedNominalSeq = nominalSelect;
			
		}else if(activeClassTab == "tabPln"){
			var $input = $("#plnInputPhone");
			var inputPatronNo = $.trim($input.val());
			var nominalSelect = $.trim($(".plnNominalSel").val());
			
			if(inputPatronNo == ""){
				alert("Masukkan Nomor Pelanggan Anda.");
				return validationResult;
			}
			
			if(inputPatronNo.length < 11){
				alert("Minimum nomor PLN yang harus Anda masukan adalah 11 angka.");
				$input.addClass("redAlert");
				return validationResult;
			}
			
			if(onlyNumber($input.get(0)) == false){
				$input.addClass("redAlert");
				return validationResult;
			}
						
			if(nominalSelect == ""){
				alert("Silahkan Pilih Nominal PLN.");
				return validationResult;
			}
			validationResult = true;
			$("#eCouponSms1").val(inputPatronNo);
			$("#eCouponSms2").val("");
			selectedNominalSeq = nominalSelect;
		}else if(activeClassTab == "tabGame"){
			var prefix = "game";
			var gameTypeSelVal = $.trim($("."+prefix+"TypeSel").val());
			var nominalSelect =  $.trim($("."+prefix+"NominalSel").val());
			
			if(gameTypeSelVal == ""){
				alert("Silahkan Pilih Jenis Voucher Game.");
				return validationResult;
			}
						
			if(nominalSelect == ""){
				alert("Silahkan Pilih Nominal.");
				return validationResult;
			}
			validationResult = true;
			$("#eCouponSms1").val("");
			$("#eCouponSms2").val("");
			selectedNominalSeq = nominalSelect;
		}else if(activeClassTab == "tabTv"){
			var prefix = "tv";
			var $input = $("#"+prefix+"InputPhone");
			var inputPatronNo = $.trim($input.val());
			var nominalSelect = $.trim($("."+prefix+"NominalSel").val());
			
			if(inputPatronNo == ""){
				alert("Masukkan Nomor Pelanggan Anda.");
				return validationResult;
			}
			
			if(inputPatronNo.length < 10){
				alert("Minimum nomor pelanggan yang harus Anda masukan adalah 10 angka.");
				$input.addClass("redAlert");
				return validationResult;
			}
						
			if(onlyNumber($input.get(0)) == false){
				$input.addClass("redAlert");
				return validationResult;
			}
						
			if(nominalSelect == ""){
				alert("Silahkan Pilih Nominal.");
				return validationResult;
			}
			validationResult = true;
			$("#eCouponSms1").val(inputPatronNo);
			$("#eCouponSms2").val("");
			selectedNominalSeq = nominalSelect;
		}else if(activeClassTab == "tabDonate"){
			var prefix = "donate";
			var dataTypeSelVal = $.trim($("."+prefix+"TypeSel").val());
			var nominalSelect =  $.trim($("."+prefix+"NominalSel").val());
			
			if(dataTypeSelVal == ""){
				alert("Silahkan Pilih Jenis Donasi.");
				return validationResult;
			}
						
			if(nominalSelect == ""){
				alert("Silahkan Pilih Nominal.");
				return validationResult;
			}
			validationResult = true;
			$("#eCouponSms1").val("");
			$("#eCouponSms2").val("");
			selectedNominalSeq = nominalSelect;
		}else if(activeClassTab == "tabAqua"){
			resetTabAqua();
			var phoneNo=$('.ponselNo').val();
			 var aquaAddress= $('input[type="hidden"][name="aquaAddress"]').val();
				
				if(phoneNo==""){
					alert("Masukkan No Handphone Anda.");
					return;
				}else if(aquaAddress==""){
					alert("Silahkan Masukkan Alamat Tujuan.");
					return;
				} 
				return true;
		}
		
		
		return validationResult;
	}
	
	function setNominalList(group,operator){
		var setNominalResult = false;
		$.ajax({
	        type: 'GET',
	        url: '/browsing/PulsaMain/getNominalList.do',
	        dataType: 'json',
	        data:{group: group,operator:operator},
	        async:   false,
	        success: function(data) {
	        	if(data!=null && data.result == "00"){
	        		var oprtNominalList = data.nominalList;	 
	        		if(group== "100"){
	        			resetPulsaPaketPln($("#pulsaInputPhone").get(0),"nominal");
	        		}else if(group=="200"){
	        			resetPulsaPaketPln($("#dataInputPhone").get(0),"nominal");
	        		}	        		
	        		
	        		for(var j=0; j < oprtNominalList.length ;j++){
						var oprtNominal = oprtNominalList[j];
						var optionHtml = "<option value='"+oprtNominal.seq+"' price='"+oprtNominal.price+"'>"+oprtNominal.option+"</option>";
						
						if(oprtNominal.group == "100"){
							$(".pulsaNominalSel").append(optionHtml);
						}else if (oprtNominal.group == "200"){
							$(".paketNominalSel").append(optionHtml);
						}else if (oprtNominal.group == "400"){
							$(".gameNominalSel").append(optionHtml);
						}else if (oprtNominal.group == "600"){
							$(".donateNominalSel").append(optionHtml);
						}								
					}	
	        		setNominalResult = true;	        		
	        	}else{
	        		alert("Produk belum bisa dibeli.");
	        	}
			},
	        error: function(xhr) {
	            alert("Ada kesalahan sistem. Silahkan hubungi customer service kami.");
	        }
	    });
		
		return setNominalResult;
	};
	
	var memDataLoaded =0;
	var totalPoint = 0;	
	var phoneVerifiedYN = "N";
	function getMemData(isAsync,isChecked){
		if(funcCheckIsLogin() && memDataLoaded == 0){			
			jQuery.ajax({
			    url: "/browsing/PulsaMain/instantPayUserData.do",
			    dataType: "json",
		        type: "GET",
		        async: isAsync
			}).done(function(response,status){		
				if(typeof response != 'undefined' && typeof response == 'object'){
					var responseResult = response;//eval("(" + response + ")");
					var resultCd = responseResult.resultCd;
					//alert(resultCd); // debug
					var msg = "";
					if(resultCd == "00") {	     
						totalPoint = response.totEftvPnt;
						phoneVerifiedYN = response.phoneVerifiedYN;
						memDataLoaded = 1;
						
						var $cboxInstPay = $(".cboxInstPay").not(":hidden");
						
						if(isChecked){
							$cboxInstPay.prop("checked",true);
							checkBuyInstStatus();
						}
						
					}else if(resultCd == "01"){
						msg = "Silahkan login terlebih dahulu.";
					}else{				
						msg = responseResult.resultMsg;
					}
					
					if(resultCd != "00" && msg != ""){
						alert(msg);
					}
					
				}else{
					alert("Error saat memproses.");
				}
				
				var $payInstLabel = $(".payInstLabel").not(":hidden");
				$payInstLabel.html("Bayar Instan");
			});
		}
	}
	var infoTimeout;
	function checkBuyInstStatus(){
		var $nominalSelect = $(".nominalSelect").not(":hidden");
		var price = ($nominalSelect.find('option:selected').val() == "") ? "0" : $nominalSelect.find('option:selected').attr("price");
		var priceNum = parseInt(price);
		var $cboxInstPay = $(".cboxInstPay").not(":hidden");
		var $buyNowBtn = $(".btnBuy").not(":hidden");
		var initCboxChecked = false;
		var validationPass= false;
		
		if(priceNum == 0){
			alert("Silahkan pilih nominal.");
			$cboxInstPay.prop("checked",false);
			return validationPass;
		}else if(funcCheckIsLogin()){
			if($cboxInstPay.is(":checked")){
				initCboxChecked = true;
				$cboxInstPay.prop("checked",false); //uncheck first, getmemdata might have delay (UX)
			}
			
			
			if(memDataLoaded == 0){	
				var $payInstLabel = $(".payInstLabel").not(":hidden");
				$payInstLabel.html("Checking...");
				getMemData(true,initCboxChecked);				
				return validationPass;
			}			
			
			if(initCboxChecked){
				$cboxInstPay.prop("checked",true);
			}
			var $instPay = $(".pls-instpay").not(":hidden");
			var $msgTop = $instPay.find(".msgTop");
			
			if(priceNum > 0 && funcCheckIsLogin() && totalPoint >= priceNum){					
				if(initCboxChecked){
					
					$buyNowBtn.html("Bayar");
					$msgTop.html("Anda akan menggunakan poin elevenia sebesar "+numberComma(priceNum)+" P").show();	
					clearTimeout(infoTimeout);
		   			infoTimeout = setTimeout(function(){
		   				$msgTop.hide();
		   			},5000);	
		   			validationPass = true;
				}else{
					$buyNowBtn.html("Beli Sekarang");
					$msgTop.html("").hide();
		    		
				}
			}else if(priceNum > 0 && funcCheckIsLogin() && totalPoint < priceNum){
				if(initCboxChecked){					
					//$cboxInstPay.prop("checked",false);
					$msgTop.html("<i class=\"iconAlert\"></i> Poin elevenia Anda tidak cukup untuk melakukan pembayaran.").show();										
					clearTimeout(infoTimeout);
		   			infoTimeout = setTimeout(function(){
		   				$msgTop.hide();
		   			},5000);
		   			$buyNowBtn.removeClass("active");
				}else{
					$buyNowBtn.html("Beli Sekarang");
					$msgTop.html("").hide();
					$buyNowBtn.addClass("active");
				}
			}else{
				$cboxInstPay.prop("checked",false);
				$buyNowBtn.html("Beli Sekarang");
				if(priceNum > 0){
					$buyNowBtn.addClass("active");
				}else{
					$buyNowBtn.removeClass("active");					
				}
			}
		}else{			
			$cboxInstPay.prop("checked",false);
		}		
		return validationPass;
	}
    </script>

    <script>
     $(function(){	
	
	isiPulsaLazyLoad();
	function isiPulsaLazyLoad(){
		$(".isiPulsaLazyLoad:visible").lazyload({
			placeholder : "/img_11ia/loading.gif"
		});
	}
	
	
	function showTopUpTab(thisTab){
		var dataClassTab= $(thisTab).data("tab");
		$('.pulsaList').find('a').removeClass('active');
		$(thisTab).addClass('active');
		
		$('.widOpt, .widBan').hide();

		$("." + dataClassTab).show();
		$("#" + dataClassTab + "Ban").show();
		
		//XOP-14177 Start
		if(dataClassTab == "gameOpt")
			$("." + dataClassTab).find(".instPay").hide();
		//XOP-14177 End
		
	}	

	
	//open default tab
	/* if($('.pulsaWidCon .pulsaList ul li a').length > 0){
		var defaultTabObj = $('.pulsaWidCon .pulsaList ul li a').eq(0);
		showTopUpTab(defaultTabObj);		
	}
	
	$('.pulsaWidCon .pulsaList ul li a').click(function(){
		showTopUpTab(this);
	}); */
	
	
	$('.pulsaNominalSel').change(function(){
		var price = ($(this).find('option:selected').val() == "") ? "Rp -" : $(this).find('option:selected').attr("price");
		if(isNaN(price) === false){
			$('.pls-price .prc').not(":hidden").html("Rp "+numberComma(price));
			$('.btn-buy').not(":hidden").addClass("active");		
		}else{
			$('.pls-price .prc').not(":hidden").html(price);
			$('.btn-buy').not(":hidden").removeClass("active");
		}		
		resetPayInstant();		
	});
	
	$('.paketNominalSel').change(function(){
		var price = ($(this).find('option:selected').val() == "") ? "Rp -" : $(this).find('option:selected').attr("price");
		if(isNaN(price) === false){
			$('.pls-price .prc').not(":hidden").html("Rp "+numberComma(price));
			$('.btn-buy').not(":hidden").addClass("active");
		}else{
			$('.pls-price .prc').removeClass("active").html(price);
			$('.btn-buy').not(":hidden").removeClass("active");
		}
		resetPayInstant();	
	});
	
	$('.plnNominalSel').change(function(){
		var price = ($(this).find('option:selected').val() == "") ? "Rp -" : $(this).find('option:selected').attr("price");
		var $btnBuy = $('.btn-buy').not(":hidden");
		var $pricePrc = $('.pls-price .prc').not(":hidden");
		if(isNaN(price) === false){
			$pricePrc.not(":hidden").html("Rp "+numberComma(price));
			
			var inputPhoneNo = $.trim($("#plnInputPhone").val());	
			
			if(inputPhoneNo != "" && isNaN(inputPhoneNo) === false){
				$btnBuy.addClass("active");
			}else{
				$btnBuy.removeClass("active");
			}			
		}else{
			$pricePrc.removeClass("active").html(price);
			$btnBuy.removeClass("active");
		}
		resetPayInstant();	
	});
	
	$('.tvNominalSel').change(function(){
		var prefix = "tv";
		var price = ($(this).find('option:selected').val() == "") ? "Rp -" : $(this).find('option:selected').attr("price");
		var $btnBuy = $('.btn-buy').not(":hidden");
		var $pricePrc = $('.pls-price .prc').not(":hidden");
		if(isNaN(price) === false){
			$pricePrc.html("Rp "+numberComma(price));
			
			var inputPhoneNo = $.trim($("#"+prefix+"InputPhone").val());	
			if(inputPhoneNo != ""  && isNaN(inputPhoneNo) === false){
				$btnBuy.addClass("active");
			}else{
				$btnBuy.removeClass("active");
			}			
		}else{
			$btnBuy.removeClass("active").html(price);
			$btnBuy.removeClass("active");
		}
		resetPayInstant();	
	});
	
	$("#pulsaInputPhone").change(function(e){
		
		var inputPhoneNo = $.trim($(this).val());		
		if(inputPhoneNo.length > 3 && checkOperatorPrefix(this) == false){
			return false;
		}else if(inputPhoneNo.length  < 3){
			resetPulsaPaketPln(this,"all");
		}else if(onlyNumber(this) == false){
			$('.pulsaBtnBuy').removeClass("active");
			
		}
	});
	

	$("#dataInputPhone").change(function(e){
		
		var inputPhoneNo = $.trim($(this).val());		
		if(inputPhoneNo.length > 3 && checkOperatorPrefix(this) == false){
			return false;
		}else if(inputPhoneNo.length < 3){
			resetPulsaPaketPln(this,"all");
		}else if(onlyNumber(this) == false){
			$('.dataBtnBuy').removeClass("active");
		}
	});	
	
	
	$("input#tagihanMemberId").keyup(function(e){
		var inpData = $.trim($(this).val());	
		if(onlyNumber(this) == false){

			$('#tagihanErr span').html("Nomor Pelanggan hanya boleh diisi angka");
			
			$('#tagihanErr').css("display","block");
			$('#tagihanErr').css("margin-left","5px");
			$('a#tagihanBtnPay').css("margin-top","0px");
			$('#tagihanMemberId').focus();
		}else{

			$('#tagihanErr span').html("");

			$('#tagihanErr').hide();

			$('a#tagihanBtnPay').css("margin-top","25px");
			
			setBillerLogo(inpData,'800');
			
			
		}
	});
	
	$("#plnInputPhone").change(function(e){		
		var inputPhoneNo = $.trim($(this).val());	
		var selectedNominal = $(".plnNominalSel").find('option:selected').val();
		if(inputPhoneNo != "" && selectedNominal != "" && onlyNumber(this) == true){
			$('.btn-buy').not(":hidden").addClass("active");
		}else{
			$('.btn-buy').not(":hidden").removeClass("active");
		}
		
		
	});
	
	
	
	$("#tvInputPhone").change(function(e){	
		var prefix = "tv";
		var inputPhoneNo = $.trim($(this).val());	
		var selectedNominal = $("."+prefix+"NominalSel").find('option:selected').val();
		var $btnBuy = $(".btn-buy").not(":hidden");
		if(inputPhoneNo != "" && selectedNominal != "" && onlyNumber(this) == true){
			$btnBuy.addClass("active");
		}else{
			$btnBuy.removeClass("active");
		}
		
		
	});
	
	$(".gameTypeSel").change(function(e){
		var operator = $(this).val();
		var group = $(this).attr("data-dtlscd");
		
		resetPulsaPaketPln(this,"nominal");
		if(operator != "" && group !=""){
			setNominalList(group,operator);		
		}
	});
	
	$('.gameNominalSel').change(function(){
		var prefix = "game";
		var price = ($(this).find('option:selected').val() == "") ? "Rp -" : $(this).find('option:selected').attr("price");
		var $pricePrc = $(".pls-price .prc").not(":hidden");
		var $btnBuy = $(".btn-buy").not(":hidden");
		if(isNaN(price) === false){
			$pricePrc.html("Rp "+numberComma(price));
			
			var input1 = $.trim($("."+prefix+"TypeSel").val());	
			if(input1 != ""){
				$btnBuy.addClass("active");
			}			
		}else{
			$pricePrc.html(price);
			$btnBuy.removeClass("active");
		}
		resetPayInstant();	
	});
	
	$(".donateTypeSel").change(function(e){
		var operator = $(this).val();
		var group = $(this).attr("data-dtlscd");
		
		resetPulsaPaketPln(this,"nominal");
		if(operator != "" && group !=""){
			setNominalList(group,operator);		
		}
	});
	
	$('.donateNominalSel').change(function(){
		var prefix = "donate";
		var price = ($(this).find('option:selected').val() == "") ? "Rp -" : $(this).find('option:selected').attr("price");
		var $pricePrc = $(".pls-price .prc").not(":hidden");
		var $btnBuy = $(".btn-buy").not(":hidden");
		if(isNaN(price) === false){
			$pricePrc.html("Rp "+numberComma(price));
			
			var input1 = $.trim($("."+prefix+"TypeSel").val());	
			if(input1 != ""){
				$btnBuy.addClass("active");
			}			
		}else{
			$pricePrc.html(price);
			$btnBuy.removeClass("active");
		}
		resetPayInstant();	
	});	

	
	$(".pls-instpay .tooltipC").hover(
			function(){
				var $msgTop = $(this).find(".msgTop");
				if($msgTop.html() == ""){
					$msgTop.html("Bayar cepat menggunakan poin elevenia.");
				}
				$msgTop.show();
			},function(){
				$(this).find(".msgTop").hide();
			});
	
	$(".cboxInstPay").click(function(){
		if(!funcCheckIsLogin()){
			$(this).prop("checked",false);
			alert("Silahkan login terlebih dahulu.");
			popUpLogin("");			
		}else{
			checkBuyInstStatus();
		}
	});
	
	/* $("#pulsa_tab li a").click(function(e){
		isiPulsaLazyLoad();
	}); */
	
	$("#pulsa_tab li a").hover(function(e){
		$(this).trigger("click");
		isiPulsaLazyLoad();
	});
	
	//populate PLN nominal
	try{
		if(typeof plnNominalJson != "undefined"){
			if(plnNominalJson.hasOwnProperty("300")){
				var plnNominalList = plnNominalJson["300"];
				for(var i=0 ; i < plnNominalList.length ;i++){
					var plnNominal = plnNominalList[i];
					var optionHtml = "<option value='"+plnNominal.seq+"' price='"+plnNominal.price+"'>"+plnNominal.option+"</option>";
					$(".plnNominalSel").append(optionHtml);
				}
			}
		}
	}catch(e){console.log(e);}
	
	try{
		if(typeof tvNominalJson != "undefined"){
			for(var key in tvNominalJson){
				if(tvNominalJson.hasOwnProperty(key)){
					var tvNominalList = tvNominalJson[key];			
					for(var i=0 ; i < tvNominalList.length ;i++){
						var tvNominal = tvNominalList[i];
						var optionHtml = "<option value='"+tvNominal.seq+"' price='"+tvNominal.price+"'>"+tvNominal.option+"</option>";
						$(".tvNominalSel").append(optionHtml);
					}
				}
			}
			
		}
	}catch(e){console.log(e);}
		
	try{
		//populate game voucher type
		if(typeof gameBoJsonArr != "undefined"){
			for(var i=0 ; i < gameBoJsonArr.length ;i++){
				var gameBoJson = gameBoJsonArr[i];
				var optionHtml = "<option value='"+gameBoJson.operator+"'>"+gameBoJson.operatorNm+"</option>";
				$(".gameTypeSel").append(optionHtml);
			}
		}
	}catch(e){console.log(e);}	
		
	try{
		//populate donation type
		if(typeof donateBoJsonArr != "undefined"){
			for(var i=0 ; i < donateBoJsonArr.length ;i++){
				var dataBoJson = donateBoJsonArr[i];
				var optionHtml = "<option value='"+dataBoJson.operator+"'>"+dataBoJson.operatorNm+"</option>";
				$(".donateTypeSel").append(optionHtml);
			}
		}
	}catch(e){console.log(e);}	
		
});

$('.aquaRadio').change(function() { 
		console.log('aqua radio changed.');
		
		var $btnBuy = $(".btn-buy").not(":hidden");
		// activate the buy button					
		$btnBuy.addClass("active");		
		
		//get checked value
		$("#ahsAquaOption").val($('.aquaRadio:checked').val());
		
		// kembalikan jumlah galon ke 1 & set harga
		// set jumlah galon = 1
		$("#txtTopUpPntAmt" + 30).val(1);
		$("#txtTopUpPntNml" + 30).val(1);
		
		// set unit price
		if ($("#aquaRefill").is(":checked")) {
// 			unitPrice = 17000;	
			unitPrice = $("#priceGalonRefill").val();
			selectedAquaProduct = "AQUA Isi Ulang";
		} else {
// 			unitPrice = 55000;
			unitPrice = $("#priceGalonNew").val();
			selectedAquaProduct = "AQUA Beli Baru";
		}
		
		// set tampilan harga 
		document.getElementById('aquaPrice').value = "Rp "
			+ numberComma(unitPrice) + "";
		$("#tabAqua .pls-price .prc").html(
				"Rp " + numberComma(unitPrice));
		
	});

var topUpPntValue = {
	limitTopUpPntAmt : Number(10000000),
	
	limitTotalPntAmt : Number(15000000),
	limitSelPntAmt	 : Number(2000000),
	selTopUpBuyerPnt : 0,
	totTopUpBuyerPnt : 0,
	resTopUpBuyerPnt: 0,
	selTotalBuyerPnt : 0
};
	
	
var fnPointUpDown = function(idx, clsf){
	var txtTopUpPntAmt = jQuery("#txtTopUpPntAmt"+idx)[0];
	var amt = Number(txtTopUpPntAmt.value);
	var $txtTopUpPntNml = $("#txtTopUpPntNml"+idx);
	var basepnt = $("#pntAmt"+idx).val();
	
	if("Increase" == clsf){
		amt = amt + 1;
		var totalPnt = amt * basepnt;
		if(totalPnt <= 2000000){
			$txtTopUpPntNml.val(numberComma(totalPnt));
			txtTopUpPntAmt.value = amt;
			this.fnSumPoint();
		}else{
			alert("Batas pengisian poin adalah 2.000.000P untuk satu kali transaksi.");
		}
		
	}else{
		amt = amt - 1;	
		var totalPnt = amt * basepnt;
		if(totalPnt >= basepnt){
			$txtTopUpPntNml.val(numberComma(totalPnt));
			txtTopUpPntAmt.value = amt;
			this.fnSumPoint();
		}else{
			alert("Batas minimum pengisian poin adalah "+numberComma(basepnt)+" P.");
		}
	}
};
jQuery(document).ready(function() {
	fnSumPoint();
	// historical
	setHistoricalPulsa();
	fnSumPointAqua();

});
var fnSumPoint = function(){
	var pntAmtType = jQuery("input[name=pntAmtType]");
	var amt = 0;
	var frmTopUp = document.frmTopUp;
	this.removeParamInput("buyerPntOrdSet");
	this.setFormParamData(frmTopUp, "buyerPntOrdSet", "0:0");
	for(var i=0,size=pntAmtType.length;i<size;i++){
		amt = amt + fnCalBuyerPnt(pntAmtType[i].value);
	}
	//topUpPntValue.totTopUpBuyerPnt = topUpPntValue.curTopUpBuyerPnt + Number(amt);
	topUpPntValue.selTopUpBuyerPnt = Number(amt);
	//topUpPntValue.selTotalBuyerPnt = topUpPntValue.totEftvPnt + Number(amt);
	//topUpPntValue.resTopUpBuyerPnt = topUpPntValue.limitTopUpPntAmt - topUpPntValue.curTopUpBuyerPnt;
	amt = amt +"";
	
	var $pricePrc = $("#tabPoin .pls-price .prc");
	if("0" != amt && Number(amt) > 0){
		//jQuery("#TopUpPntTotalPrc").html("Rp " + numberComma(amt));
		$pricePrc.html("Rp "+numberComma(amt));
	}else{
		//jQuery("#TopUpPntTotalPrc").html("Rp 0");
		$pricePrc.html("Rp -");
	}
	
	
};

var fnSumPointAqua = function(){
	
	var txtTopUpPntAmt = jQuery("#txtTopUpPntAmt30")[0];
	var amt = Number(txtTopUpPntAmt.value);
	
	var $pricePrc = $("#tabAqua .pls-price .prc");
// 	if("0" != amt && Number(amt*17000) > 0){
	if("0" != amt && Number(amt* $("#priceGalonRefill").val()) > 0){
		//jQuery("#TopUpPntTotalPrc").html("Rp " + numberComma(amt));
		$pricePrc.html("Rp "+numberComma(amt*$("#priceGalonRefill").val()));
	}else{
		//jQuery("#TopUpPntTotalPrc").html("Rp 0");
// 		$pricePrc.html("Rp 17.000");

		$pricePrc.html("Rp "+$("#priceGalonRefill").val());
	}
	
	
};

var setFormParamData = function(obj, inputNm, values) {

	if ("string" == (typeof values) || "String" == (typeof values)) {
		jQuery("<input type='hidden'/>").attr({
			name : inputNm,
			value : values
		}).appendTo(obj);
	} else if ("number" == (typeof values) || "Nember" == (typeof values)) {
		jQuery("<input type='hidden'/>").attr({
			name : inputNm,
			value : values
		}).appendTo(obj);
	} else if ("object" == (typeof values) || "Object" == (typeof values)) {
		for ( var i = 0, size = values.length; i < size; i++) {
			jQuery("<input type='hidden'/>").attr({
				name : inputNm,
				value : values[i]
			}).appendTo(obj);
		}
	}
};

var removeParamInput = function(name) {
	jQuery("[name=" + name + "]").each(function() {
		jQuery(this).remove();
	});
};

var fnCalBuyerPnt = function(buyerPntNo){
	var reVal = 0;
	var pntSelPrc = jQuery("#pntSelPrc"+buyerPntNo)[0].value;
	var buyerPntAmount = jQuery("#txtTopUpPntAmt"+buyerPntNo)[0].value;
	if(Number(buyerPntAmount) > 0){
		var frmTopUp = document.frmTopUp;
		this.setFormParamData(frmTopUp, "buyerPntOrdSet", ""+buyerPntNo+":"+buyerPntAmount);
		reVal = Number(pntSelPrc) * Number(buyerPntAmount);
	}
	return reVal;
};

var fnTopupPntValidation = function(){
	var reVal = false;
	
	if(!jQuery('#poinBuyTncCheck').attr('checked')){
		alert("Silahkan menyetujui perjanjian isi ulang poin.");
		return reVal;
	}
	
	if(topUpPntValue.selTopUpBuyerPnt <= 0){
		alert("Silakan pilih poin.");
		return reVal;
	}
	
	var url = location.protocol + "//www.elevenia.co.id/loyalty/AuthMallPointGiftDtls/validateTopUpPoint.do?";
	//var param = "selTopUpBuyerPnt=" + topUpPntValue.selTopUpBuyerPnt;
	var param = $("#frmTopUp").serialize();
	
	var ajaxValidatePass = false;
	jQuery.ajax({
	    url: url + param,
	    dataType: "json",
        type: "POST",
        async:false
	}).done(function(response,status){		
		if(typeof response != 'undefined' && typeof response == 'object'){
			var responseResult = response;//eval("(" + response + ")");
			var resultCd = responseResult.resultCd;
			//alert(resultCd); // debug
			var msg = "";
			if(resultCd == "00") {	     
				msg = "";	
				ajaxValidatePass = true;
			}else if(resultCd == "01"){
				msg = "Silahkan login terlebih dahulu.";
			}else{				
				msg = responseResult.resultMsg;
			}
			
			if(resultCd != "00" && msg != ""){
				alert(msg);
			}
			
		}else{
			alert("Error saat memproses.");
			//return reVal;
		}
		
	});
	if(ajaxValidatePass == true){
		reVal = true;
	}else{
		reVal = false;
	}	
	return reVal;
}

var fnTopUpSubmit = function(){
	
	if(!funcCheckIsLogin()){
		alert("Silahkan login terlebih dahulu.");
		popUpLogin("point-refill");
		return false;
	}
	if(!fnTopupPntValidation()){
		return false;
	}
	
	
	var frmTopUp = document.frmTopUp;
	frmTopUp.action = _SSL_ACTION_CONTEXT_URL_ + "/loyalty/AuthMallPointGiftDtls/getPointOrderInfo.do?isSSL=Y";
	frmTopUp.submit();
}

var fnPointUpDownAqua = function(idx, clsf){
	var txtTopUpPntAmt = jQuery("#txtTopUpPntAmt"+idx)[0];
	var amt = Number(txtTopUpPntAmt.value);
	var $txtTopUpPntNml = $("#txtTopUpPntNml"+idx);
	var basepnt = $("#pntAmt"+idx).val();
	
	var unitPrice = 0;
	
	if ($("#aquaRefill").is(":checked")) {
// 		unitPrice = 17000;
		unitPrice = $("#priceGalonRefill").val();
	} else if ($("#aquaNew").is(":checked"))  {
// 		unitPrice = 55000;
		unitPrice = $("#priceGalonNew").val();
	} else {
		$("#tabAqua .pls-price .prc").html(
				"Rp - ");
		return;
	}
	
	if("Increase" == clsf){
		if ( amt < 20 ) {
			amt = amt + 1;
			var totalPnt = amt * basepnt;
			var totalprice= amt*unitPrice;
			$txtTopUpPntNml.val(numberComma(totalPnt));
			txtTopUpPntAmt.value = amt;
			document.getElementById('aquaPrice').value ="Rp "+ numberComma(totalprice)+"";
			$("#tabAqua .pls-price .prc").html("Rp "+numberComma(totalprice));
		} else {
			console.log("Jumlah galon maksimum 20.");
			//return;										
		}
	}else{
		amt = amt - 1;	
		if(amt>=1){
			var totalPnt = amt * basepnt;
			var totalprice= amt*unitPrice;
			$txtTopUpPntNml.val(numberComma(totalPnt));
			txtTopUpPntAmt.value = amt;
			document.getElementById('aquaPrice').value ="Rp "+ numberComma(totalprice)+"";
			$("#tabAqua .pls-price .prc").html("Rp "+numberComma(totalprice));
		} else {
			// jika kurang dari satu, tidak lakukan apa-apa
			// alert("Minimal satu");
			console.log("Jumlah galon isi ulang minimal 1.")
		}

		

	}
};
var popupTermNCondition = function(){
	var popupUrl = _ACTION_CONTEXT_URL_+"/html/bp/skn/guide/TnC-popup.html"
	
	var screenWidth = screen.availwidth;
	var screenHeight = screen.availheight;
	var intWidth=620, intHeight=700, intLeft = 'auto', intTop = 'auto', vScrollbars = '1', vResizable = '0', vStatus = '0';
	if(intWidth >= screenWidth){
		intWidth = screenWidth - 40;
		vScrollbars = 1;
	}
	if(intHeight >= screenHeight){
		intHeight = screenHeight - 40;
		intWidth = intWidth + 20;
		vScrollbars = 1;
	}
	if(intLeft == 'auto' || intTop == 'auto'){
		var intLeft = (screenWidth - intWidth) / 2;
		var intTop = (screenHeight - intHeight) / 2;
	}

	var optionVal = eval("'width=" + intWidth + ",height=" + intHeight + ",left=" + intLeft + ",top=" + intTop + ",scrollbars=" + vScrollbars + ",resizable=" + vResizable + ",status=" + vStatus + "'");
	
	var newwindow = window.open(popupUrl,'popupTermNCondition',optionVal);
	if (window.focus){
		newwindow.focus();
	}
	return false;
};

function SearchMapOpen() {
    var prov = "DKI JAKARTA";
    var city = "Jakarta Pusat Kota Administrasi Jakarta Pusat DKI JAKARTA";
    var phoneNo= $('.ponselNo').val();
	
    if(!funcCheckIsLogin()){
    	alert("Silahkan login terlebih dahulu.");
		openLoginPopup('02');	
	}else{
    
	    if(phoneNo!="")    
		{
			  $.ajax({
			      url: "/register/personalinfomation/serviceAreaChk.do",
			      type: "POST",
			      data: {prov:prov, city:city},
			      datatype: "json",
			      success : function(response, status, request) {
			        if (prov=="" || city=="" /*|| $("#rcvrDtlsAddr").val()==""*/) {
			          alert("Mohon isi alamat lengkap terlebih dahulu");
			        } else if (!response) {
			          alert("Layanan same day tidak tersedia di daerah Anda");
			        } else {
			          var json = eval("("+response+")");
			          
			          if($('#hdnLat_SD, #hdnLng_SD').val()=="") {
			            $('#hdnLat_SD').val(json.lat); $('#hdnLng_SD').val(json.lng);
			          }
			          $('body').addClass('overH');
			          $('#loadingCheckOut').show();
			          
			          if($("#hdnLat_SD").val() != "" && $("#hdnLng_SD").val() != "") {
			            $("#ifrmGoogleMap").attr("src", "/jsp/order/order/incGoogleMapSearchBox.jsp?lat=" + $("#hdnLat_SD").val() + "&lng=" + $("#hdnLng_SD").val()+ "&type=AQUAV3"+"&phoneNo=" + phoneNo  );
			          }
			          $('#ifrmGoogleMap').css('top', ($(window).height()-$('#ifrmGoogleMap').height())/2 + "px");
			          $('#ifrmGoogleMap').css('left', ($(window).width()-$('#ifrmGoogleMap').width())/2 + "px");
			          $("#ifrmGoogleMap").show();
			        }
			      },
			      error: function(data) {
			        alert("Failed.");
			      }
			    });
		}else
		{
			alert("masukkan nomor telpon ");	
		}
	}
  
  }
  
function validatePhoneNoAqua(thisSel,event){
	var inputPhoneNo = $.trim(thisSel.value);
	var firstTwoPrefix = inputPhoneNo.substring(0,2);
	var firstThreePrefix = inputPhoneNo.substring(0,3);
	
	if(onlyNumber(thisSel) == false){
		return false;
	}
	 $('#pulsaBtnBuyAqua').removeClass("active");
	 $('input[type="hidden"][name="aquaAddress"]').val('');
	if((firstTwoPrefix == "08" && firstThreePrefix!="080" ) ||firstThreePrefix == "628" )
	{
		$("#idProvince_chosen").html("<a href=\"javascript:SearchMapOpen();\"><p class=\"icon-location\"></p><span class=\"text-location\">Pilih Lokasi Tujuan Pada Peta</span><p class=\"icon-chevron\"></p></a>");
		$("#noteAdress").css("display","block");
		$(thisSel).removeClass("redAlert");
	}else
	{
		$("#idProvince_chosen").html("<a href=\"#\"><p class=\"icon-location\"></p><span class=\"text-location\">Pilih Lokasi Tujuan Pada Peta</span><p class=\"icon-chevron\"></p></a>");
		$("#noteAdress").css("display","none");
		$(thisSel).addClass("redAlert");
		return false;
	}

	/*if(event.keyCode != 8 && event.keyCode != 46 && tempPhoneNo != inputPhoneNo){
		if((inputPhoneNo.length == 4 || (inputPhoneNo.length == 5 && firstTwoPrefix == "62") || (inputPhoneNo.length == 3 && firstThreePrefix == "999")) ){
			return false;
		}
	}else if(inputPhoneNo.length < 3 || (firstTwoPrefix == "08" && inputPhoneNo.length < 4) || (firstTwoPrefix == "62" && inputPhoneNo.length < 5)){
		resetPulsaPaketPln(thisSel,"all");
	}*/
	
	tempPhoneNo = inputPhoneNo;
}

function afterAquaAgreement2(){
 var form = document.frmMain;
 var optionStock= document.getElementById('txtTopUpPntNml30').value;
 var noteAddr= $("#ifrmGoogleMapAHS").contents().find("#spanAddress").val();
 var aquaDlvNote= $("#ifrmGoogleMapAHS").contents().find("#aquaDlvNote").val();
 var aquaPhoneNo = $("#ifrmGoogleMapAHS").contents().find("#aquaPhoneNo").val();
 
 var optTyp = $(".aquaRadio:checked").val();

 
 document.getElementsByName("optionStock")[0].value = optionStock;
 document.getElementsByName("aquaPhoneNo")[0].value = aquaPhoneNo;
 document.getElementsByName("noteAddr")[0].value = noteAddr;
 document.getElementsByName("aquaDlvNote")[0].value = aquaDlvNote;
 
$.ajax({
	type :"GET",
	url:"/browsing/promotion/serverCurrentDateTimeAjax.do",
	dataType:"json"
}).done(function(data){
	console.log(data.currentDateTime);
	var currentDateTime= data.currentDateTime;
	var endDateTime= '2016-12-14-17-59-59'
	
	// --- Init Timer Period ---

	var jdateParts2= currentDateTime.split("-");
	var vdateTime = parseInt(jdateParts2[3]);
//	var vdateTimeMin = parseInt(jdateParts2[4]); 
//	var vdateDay = parseInt(jdateParts2[2]);

	if (vdateTime > 23 || vdateTime<6) { 
		alert("sudah lewat jam");
		return false;
    }else
    {
    			$.ajax({
    		        type: 'GET',
    		        url: '/browsing/PulsaMain/getAquaProductDetail.do',
    		        data : {
    		        	prdId: optTyp
    		        },
    		        dataType: 'json',
    		        success: function(data) {
    		        	if(data!=null && data.result == "00"){
    		        		//set parameter
							 var ahsName= $('input[type="hidden"][name="ahsName"]').val();
							 var ahsId= $('input[type="hidden"][name="ahsId"]').val();
							 var ahsLat= $('input[type="hidden"][name="ahsLat"]').val();
							 var ahsLong= $('input[type="hidden"][name="ahsLong"]').val();
							 var aquaAddress= $('input[type="hidden"][name="aquaAddress"]').val();
							 var accessToken=$('input[type="hidden"][name="accessToken"]').val();
							 var hdnLng_SD= $('input[type="hidden"][name="hdnLng_SD"]').val();
							 var hdnLat_SD= $('input[type="hidden"][name="hdnLat_SD"]').val();
							 var optionStock= $('input[type="hidden"][name="optionStock"]').val();
							 var ahsAddr= $('input[type="hidden"][name="ahsAddr"]').val();
							 var ahsPhone= $('input[type="hidden"][name="ahsPhone"]').val();
							 
    						form.elements.prdNo.value =  data.prdNo;
    						form.elements.mstrPrdNo.value =  data.mstrPrdNo;
    						form.elements.selMthdCd.value =  data.selMthdCd;
    						form.elements.dispCtgrNo.value =  data.dispCtgrNo;
    						form.elements.ldispCtgrNo.value =  data.ldispCtgrNo;
    						form.elements.bsnDealClf.value =  data.bsnDealClf;
    						form.elements.optCnt.value =  "1";
    						form.elements.optionStock.value = optionStock;//QUANTITY
    						form.elements.selMnbdNo.value =  data.selMnbdNo;
    						form.elements.mobileYn.value =  data.mobileYn;
    						form.elements.selPrc.value =  data.selPrc;
    						form.elements.iscpn.value =  data.iscpn;
    						form.elements.selStatCd.value =  data.selStatCd;
    						form.elements.optionStckNo.value =  data.optionStckNo;
    						form.elements.optionPrc.value =  data.optionPrc;
    						form.elements.optionStockHid.value =  data.optionStockHid;
    						form.elements.dlvDtlsMthdCd.value =  data.dlvDtlsMthdCd;
    						form.elements.dlvMthdCd.value =  data.dlvMthdCd;
    						form.elements.optionStockHid.value =  data.totStock;
    						form.elements.optionStckNo.value =  data.totPrdStckNo;
    						form.elements.optionPrc.value =  data.totPrdPrc;
    						form.elements.prdMinorYn.value =  data.prdMinorYn;
    					
    						
    						form.elements.ahsName.value=ahsName;
    						form.elements.ahsId.value=ahsId;
    						form.elements.ahsLat.value=ahsLat;
    						form.elements.ahsLong.value=ahsLong;
    						form.elements.aquaAddress.value=aquaAddress;
    						form.elements.accessToken.value=accessToken;
    						form.elements.optionStock.value=optionStock;
    						form.elements.hdnLng_SD.value=hdnLng_SD;
    						form.elements.hdnLat_SD.value=hdnLat_SD; 
    						form.elements.aquaPhoneNo.value=aquaPhoneNo; 
    						form.elements.ahsAddr.value=ahsAddr; 
    						form.elements.ahsPhone.value=ahsPhone; 
    						form.elements.noteAddr.value=noteAddr; 
    						form.elements.aquaDlvNote.value=aquaDlvNote;
    						
    						//submit!
							form.action = _SSL_ACTION_CONTEXT_URL_ + "/pay/newOrderStep1/getOrderInfo.do";
							form.elements.isFast.value = "Y";
							form.elements.isPopup.value = "N";
							form.elements.isSSL.value = "Y";
							
							if($(".cboxInstPay").not(":hidden").is(":checked")){
								form.elements.payInstantYN.value = "Y";
								if(phoneVerifiedYN == "Y"){
									
									topUpBuyNowInstPay();	
									
								}else{
									form.elements.phoneVerifiedYN.value = "N";
									form.submit();
								}										
							}else{
								form.elements.payInstantYN.value = "N";
								form.submit();
							}
							
			        	}else if(data!=null && data.result == "01"){ //XOP-11785
			        		alert(data.msg);
			        		buyTopUpProcessing = false;
			        		location.href=data.redirectUrl;
			        	}else{
			        		alert(data.msg);
			        		buyTopUpProcessing = false;
			        	}
    				},
    		        error: function(xhr) {
    		            alert("Ada kesalahan sistem. Silahkan hubungi customer service kami.");
    		            buyTopUpProcessing = false;	
    		        }
    		    });
    		
    	}
    
    
});

}

var afterAquaAgreement3= function(){
	$("#ifrmGoogleMapAHS").contents().find("#isPayAquaBtnPress").val("Y");
	document.getElementById("ifrmGoogleMapAHS").contentWindow.setMarkerAfterPressPay(); 

};

function AfterAquaAgreementMaster(){
	if( $("#ifrmGoogleMapAHS").contents().find("#isPayAquaBtnPressPay").val() != 'Y'){
		return;
	}
	var deff = $.Deferred();
	var deffFunc = deff.promise();
	deffFunc.done(afterAquaAgreement3).done(afterAquaAgreement3P2);
	deff.resolve();
}

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var msgLength = 0;
	function clearconsole()
	{ 
	  console.log(window.console);  
	  if(window.console )
	  {    
	    console.clear();  
	  }
	}
	
	
	function getAwsProductRecommendationFront(){
		
		var apiUrl ='http://api.elevenia.co.id/rest/productRecommendation/front';
	
	
		var memNoVar ='0';
		
		var displayRecommendation= 'Y';
	
		
		if(apiUrl !='' && apiUrl!=null && memNoVar !='' && memNoVar!=null && null !=displayRecommendation && 'Y'==displayRecommendation){
			
				
				$.ajax({
					  url: '/getProductRecommendation',
					  type: "GET",
					  async: true,
					  success : function(result){
						  var resultX =result;
						  var  msgLength= 0;
						  try{
						 	 msgLength = resultX.msgContent.length;
						 	 	  
						  }	catch(err){}
					
						  if(msgLength && msgLength>=6){
							  
							  
					var s ="";
							s+="  	  <div class='span12' style='margin-left:0px !important;width:1190px !important'>";
							  s+="<div class='main-section' id='product_recommendation_aws'>";
								  s+="			<div class='sec-title'>";
									  s+="			<h2>Rekomendasi untuk Anda</h2>";
										  s+="	</div>";
											  s+="<div class='card no-pad'>";
												  s+="<div class='swiper-container main-swiper swiper-container-horizontal' id='prodcut_recommendation_aws'>";
													  s+=" <div class='swiper-wrapper' style=''></div>";
														  s+="<ul class='arrow-nav' >";
															  s+="<li class='li_prev'><a href='javascript:void(0);' class='sp-main' style='top:120px;'>&lt;</a></li>";
															  s+="<li class='li_next'><a href='javascript:void(0);' class='sp-main' style='top:120px;'>&gt;</a></li>";
															  s+="</ul>";
													 s+="</div>";
																			  s+="		</div>";
																				  s+="		</div>";
																					  s+="		</div>";
																					 
							  $('#product_recommendation_aws_scarab_container').append(s);
							  
							  
							  var sSub ="";
									$.each(resultX.msgContent, function (index, item) {
								        var price =item.price;
								        var imgUrlSecure = item.zoom_image;
								        var LinkSecure = item.link;
								        price = price.substring(0,price.indexOf("."));
								        
								        
								        
								        sSub+="		<div class='swiper-slide swp-prd no-translate '>	";
								        	sSub+="		<a href='"+LinkSecure+"' id='"+item.rank_id+"'  data-scarabitem='"+ item.rank_id+ "'" + "class='dm_sp_user_reco' >	";
								        		sSub+="		<p class='prd-img'>	";
								        			sSub+="		<img class='prdRecAwsLazy' data-original='"+imgUrlSecure+"' alt='"+item.title+"' onerror='this.src=CommonImage.getNoimgUrl(_SSL_IMG_URL_, 170);' style='background-repeat: no-repeat; background-position: center center; display: inline;' width='170' height='170'>";
								        			sSub+="	</p>";
								        			sSub+="<p class='prd-title notranslate'>"+item.title+"</p>		";
								        			sSub+="<p class='prd-price-b notranslate'></p>";
								        					sSub+="<p class='prd-price notranslate'><strong> "+ moneyFormat.format(price)+"</strong></p>";
								        			sSub+="	</a>";
								        	sSub+="</div>	";
								        	
								    });
								     $('#product_recommendation_aws_scarab_container .swiper-wrapper').append(sSub);
								     
										initPrdRecAwsPersonalSwiper();
						  }
					  },
					  error : function(XMLHttpRequest, status, err) {
						  console.error("error on:"+ err.toString());
					  }
					});
		}
		
	}
	
	
	
	function showRecommendationLazyLoad(){
	
		 $(".swiper-slide-visible .prdRecAwsLazy:visible").lazyload({
				placeholder : "/img_11ia/loading.gif"
				,load: function(elements_left, settings){				
				}
			});
	}
	function initPrdRecAwsPersonalSwiper(){
		var swiperObject=new Swiper($("#prodcut_recommendation_aws"), {
		     slidesPerView: 6,
		     slidesPerGroup: 2,
		     spaceBetween: 0,
		     speed: 0,
		     watchSlidesVisibility: true,
		     nextButton: '.arrow-nav .li_next',
		     prevButton: '.arrow-nav .li_prev',
		     loop:true
		     ,onSlideNextEnd:function(){
		    	 showRecommendationLazyLoad();
		     }
			 ,onSlidePrevEnd:function(){
				 showRecommendationLazyLoad();
		     }			
		});
	}

     <script type="text/javascript">
      var baseUrl;
	if(location.protocol=="https:"){
 		baseUrl = "https://"+document.domain;
 	}else{
 		baseUrl= "http://"+document.domain;
 	}
 	
	 /* Main page announcment XOP-4067 */
	 $(function(){
			$.ajax({
				type: "GET",
				url: baseUrl+"/wingR/WingRBannerAction/getAnnouncement.do",
				dataType: 'json'
				
			}).done(function( response ) {	
				var html="";
				jsonArr 	= response.announcment;
				var general = response.general;
				var system = response.system;
				var event = response.event;
				//alert(jsonArr);
				//alert(jsonArr.length);
				if(jsonArr.length > 0){
					for(var i=0; i <jsonArr.length;i++){
						var jsonObj	 	 = jsonArr[i];
						var annNO		 = jsonObj.ntceNo;
						var annTitle 	 = jsonObj.title;
						var annDate		 = jsonObj.createDt;
						
						var annClsGubun  = "red";
						var annStrGubun  = "";
						
						if(jsonObj.gubun == "01"){
							annClsGubun = "red";
							strGubun    = general;
						}else if(jsonObj.gubun == "02"){
							annClsGubun = "";
							strGubun = system;
						}else if(jsonObj.gubun == "04"){
							annClsGubun = "org";
							strGubun    = event;
						}
						//html+= "<li><span>"+annNO+"</span><em class="+annClsGubun+">"+strGubun+"</em><a onclick=\"javascript:detailNotice('"+annNO+"');\" href=\"javascript:detailNotice('"+annNO+"');\">"+annTitle+"</a><i>"+annDate+"</i></li>";
						html+= "<li><i>"+annDate+"</i><a onclick=\"javascript:detailNotice('"+annNO+"');\" href=\"javascript:detailNotice('"+annNO+"');\">"+annTitle+"</a></li>";
					}
					$("#announcment").html(html);
				}else{
					$("#bodyAnnouncment").html('');
				}
			});
	});

	function detailNotice(ntceNo){
		var url;
		if(location.protocol=="https:"){
	 		url = "https://www.elevenia.co.id/helpdesk/Notice/getDetailNotice.do?ntceNo="+ntceNo;
	 	}else{
	 		url = "http://www.elevenia.co.id/helpdesk/Notice/getDetailNotice.do?ntceNo="+ntceNo;
	 	}
		
		jQuery('#noticeLayer').css({"display":"block", "z-index": "1000"});
		jQuery("#qnaForm").attr({
			"method": "post"
			, "target": "noticeLayer"
			, "action": url
		}).submit();
	}

	function resizeIframe(top, left, info) {
			jQuery(info.target).css({
				 "width" : info.width + "px"
				, "height" : info.height + "px"
				, "marginTop" : - (info.height/2)
				, "marginLeft" : - (info.width/2)
			}).show();
		}
		
		function closeLayer() {
			jQuery("#noticeLayer", document).attr("src", "about:blank").css({"width" : 0, "height" : 0});
			jQuery('.dimmed').remove();
			jQuery('body').removeClass('overH');
		}

     <script type="text/javascript">
      var baseUrl = "https://"+document.domain;
 	if(location.protocol=="https:"){
 		baseUrl = "https://"+document.domain;
 	}
 	
	$(function(){
		
		$.ajax({
			type: "GET",
			url: baseUrl+"/html/elevenia-blog-json.html",
			dataType: 'json'
			
		}).done(function( response ) {			
			for (var key in response) {
				var html="";
				var jsonArr = response[key];
				if(jsonArr.length > 0){
					for(var i=0; i <jsonArr.length;i++){
						var jsonObj=jsonArr[i];
						var title= jsonObj.title;
						var link= jsonObj.link;
						html+="<li><a href=\""+link+"\" title=\""+title+"\">"+title+"</a></li>";
					}
					if(key == "news_event"){
						$("#news_event").html(html);
					}else if(key=="whats_hot"){
						$("#whats_hot").html(html);
					}else if(key == "media_room"){
						$("#media_room").html(html);
					}
					
				}
			}
		});
 
		$("#schWord2").keypress(function(event) {
		    if (event.which == 13) {
		        event.preventDefault();
		        helpdeskSearch2();
		    }
		});


	});
	
	function helpdeskSearch2(){
	    var keyword = $("#schWord2").val();
	    if(keyword == ""){
	        //  !
	        alert('Masukan kata yang mau di cari.');
	        $("#schWord2").focus();
	        return;
	    }else{
	        if(keyword.length > 256){
	            //  256    .
	            alert('Pencarian permintaan tidak dapat lebih dari 256 kata._');
	            $("#schWord2").focus();
	            return;
	        };
	
	        if(InvalidXSS2(keyword)){
	            alert(" script,style,iframe,object,embed,form,img    .");
	            //  replace
	            $("#schWord2").val(replaceXSS(keyword));
	            $("#schWord2").focus();
	            return false;
	        }
	    }
	    $("#dispKwd2").val($("#schWord2").val());
	    var kwd = encodeURIComponent(encodeURIComponent($("#schWord2").val()));
	    $("#searchKeyword2").val(kwd);
	    $("#currentPage2").val("1");
	    $("#searchType2").val("K");            //   ( or  : M,  : S,  : K)
	    $("#searchForm2").attr("action",baseUrl+"/helpdesk/Category/goHelpMiddleCategory.do").submit();
	
	}
	// XSS validation
	function InvalidXSS2(val){
	    //   
	    var _REP_TAGS_ = "script|style|iframe|object|embed|form|img";
	    var _REGEX_REPTAGS = new RegExp("<(\\s*\/?\\s*("+_REP_TAGS_+")[^>]*\\s*)>","igm");
	
	    var testStr = val;
	    return _REGEX_REPTAGS.test(testStr);
	}

$(function(){
	var excerptSelector = $(".seoTextContainer #excerpt");
	var excerptContentSelector = $(".seoTextContainer #excerptContent");
	
	excerptContentSelector.show();
	
	if(typeof PAGE_KIND != 'undefined' && PAGE_KIND == "MAIN"){
		
	}else {
		if(excerptSelector.length > 0 && excerptContentSelector.length > 0){
			excerptSelector.append("<span class='seoMore notranslate'>more <span class='arrow'></span></span>");
			excerptContentSelector.append("<span class='seoLess notranslate'>less <span class='arrow'></span></span>");
			$(".seoMore").click(function(){
				$(".seoMore").hide();
				excerptContentSelector.show();
			});
			$(".seoLess").click(function(){
			
				$(".seoMore").show();
				excerptContentSelector.hide();
			});
			$(".seoMore").hide();
			//console.log("1");
		} else {
	
				//console.log("2");
			excerptContentSelector.show();
			excerptContentSelector.append("<span class='seoLess notranslate'>less <span class='arrow'></span></span>");
			$(".seoLess").click(function(){
				$(".seoMore").show();
				excerptContentSelector.hide();
			});
			
		} 
	}

	
});
